When the Ukrainian invasion began, the ballet great left a show at the Bolshoi in protest. Here he reconsiders his past ties with Russia and the silence of the cultural elite in the country of his                         // Used to toggle data-link-name on label buttons
                        var navInputCheckbox = document.getElementById('top-nav-input-checkbox')
                        var showMoreButton = document.getElementById('show-more-button')
                        var veggieBurger = document.getElementById('veggie-burger')
                        var expandedMenuClickableTags = document.querySelectorAll('.selectableMenuItem')
                        var expandedMenu = document.getElementById('expanded-menu-root')

                        // We assume News is the 1st column
                        var firstColLabel = document.getElementById('News-button')
                        var firstColLink = document.querySelectorAll('#newsLinks > li:nth-of-type(2) > a')[0]

                        var focusOnFirstNavElement = function(){
                          // need to focus on first element in list, firstColLabel is not viewable on desktop
                          if(window.getComputedStyle(firstColLabel).display === 'none'){
                            firstColLink.focus()
                          } else {
                            firstColLabel.focus()
                          }
                        }

						if (!navInputCheckbox) return; // Sticky nav replaces the nav so element no longer exists for users in test.

                        navInputCheckbox.addEventListener('click',function(){
                          document.body.classList.toggle('nav-is-open')

                          if(!navInputCheckbox.checked) {
							firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false')
                            showMoreButton.setAttribute('data-link-name','nav2 : veggie-burger : show')
                            veggieBurger.setAttribute('data-link-name','nav2 : veggie-burger : show')
                            expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach(function($selectableElement){
                                $selectableElement.setAttribute('tabindex','-1')
                            })
                          } else {
							firstColLabel.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true')
                            showMoreButton.setAttribute('data-link-name','nav2 : veggie-burger : hide')
                            veggieBurger.setAttribute('data-link-name','nav2 : veggie-burger : hide')
                            expandedMenuClickableTags.forEach(function($selectableElement){
                                $selectableElement.setAttribute('tabindex','0')
                            })
                            focusOnFirstNavElement()
                          }
                        })
                        var toggleMainMenu = function(e){
                          navInputCheckbox.click()
                        }
                        // Close hide menu on press enter
                        var keydownToggleMainMenu = function(e){
                          // keyCode: 13 => Enter key | keyCode: 32 => Space key
                          if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 32) {
                            e.preventDefault()
                            toggleMainMenu()
                          }
                        }
                        showMoreButton.addEventListener('keydown', keydownToggleMainMenu)
                        veggieBurger.addEventListener('keydown', keydownToggleMainMenu)
                        // Accessibility to hide Nav when pressing escape key
                        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
                          // keyCode: 27 => esc
                          if (e.keyCode === 27) {
                            if(navInputCheckbox.checked) {
                              toggleMainMenu()
                              if(window.getComputedStyle(veggieBurger).display === 'none'){
                                showMoreButton.focus()
                              }else{
                                veggieBurger.focus()
                              }
                            }
                          }
                        })
                        // onBlur close dialog
                        document.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e){
                          if(navInputCheckbox.checked && !expandedMenu.contains(e.target)){
                            toggleMainMenu()
                          }
                        });
                      })</script><div data-component="nav2" class="dcr-1yaxlqk"><input type="checkbox" id="top-nav-input-checkbox" name="more" tabIndex="-1" aria-hidden="true" role="button" data-ignore="global-link-styling" class="dcr-t8badk"><span class="dcr-61wgh1">03.11 AEST</span></a></div><h2 class="dcr-e6uddv">Ten bodies recovered from scene of plane crash, say Russian investigators</h2></header><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Russian investigators said Friday they had recovered flight recorders and 10 bodies from the scene of a plane crash thought to have killed Wagner chief <strong>Yevgeny Prigozhin</strong> two days ago.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">An investigation is underway into what caused Wednesday’s crash, which came exactly two months after Wagner’s short-lived rebellion against Moscow’s military leadership.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">“In the course of initial investigative work, the bodies of 10 victims were found at the site of the plane crash,” Russia’s Investigative Committee said on social media.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">“Molecular genetic analyses are being carried out to establish their identities,” it said, adding that “flight &lt;li>&lt;p>The Kremlin said on Friday that western suggestions that the Wagner group boss, &lt;a href=\&quot;https://www.theguardian.com/world/yevgeny-prigozhin\&quot; data-component=\&quot;auto-linked-tag\&quot;>Yevgeny Prigozhin&lt;/a>, had been killed on its orders were an “absolute lie”, and it declined to definitively confirm his death, citing the need to wait for test results.&lt;/p>&lt;/li>\n &lt;li>&lt;p>Russian investigators have confirmed the death of the pilot of the plane that crashed with the loss of all onboard including Prigozhin, according to a source with knowledge of the matter.&lt;/p>&lt;/li>\n &lt;li>&lt;p>German prosecutors say they are investigating the attempted murder of Berlin-based Russian journalist Elena Kostyuchenko after she was one of three Russian-exile journalists who experienced symptoms consistent with poisoning.&lt;/p>&lt;/li>\n &lt;li>&lt;p>Poland’s domestic security agency is investigating whether an outbreak of legionnaires’ disease that has killed seven people in the south of the country could be the result of intentional tampering with the water system, authorities said on Friday.&lt;/p>&lt;/li>\n &lt;li>&lt;p>The UK’s defence ministry has said there is not yet definitive proof&lt;strong> Prigozhin&lt;/strong> was onboard a plane that crashed with no survivors earlier this week but it is “highly likely” he is dead, Reuters reports.&lt;/p>&lt;/li>\n &lt;li>&lt;p>The US state department on Thursday imposed sanctions on 13 people and entities it said were reportedly connected to the AEST</span></a></div><h2 class="dcr-e6uddv">Here is a summary of today's developments</h2></header><ul class="dcr-1kas69x">
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The Belarusian president, Alexander Lukashenko, said on Friday that he had warned the Wagner group chiefs <strong>Yevgeny Prigozhin</strong> and Dmitry Utkin – who apparently died in a plane crash earlier this week – to watch out for possible threats to their lives, and he insisted that Wagner fighters would remain in Belarus.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">A second plane linked to Prigozhin by some Russian media has no connection to Wagner group and never did, the CEO of the aircraft operator company told Reuters.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Russian investigators said on Friday that they had recovered flight recorders and 10 bodies from the scene of a plane crash thought to have killed Prigozhin two days ago.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Heineken has completed its lengthy exit from <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/russia" data-link-name="in body link">Russia</a> with the sale of its operations there for a symbolic €1, after Moscow clamped down on asset sales in retaliation for western sanctions.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The Kremlin said on Friday that western suggestions that Yevgeny Prigozhin had been killed on its orders were an “absolute lie”. It declined to definitively confirm his death, citing the need to wait for test results.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The UK’s defence ministry has said there is not yet definitive proof that<strong> </strong>Prigozhin was onboard the plane that crashed with no survivors earlier this week, but said it is “highly likely” he is dead, Reuters reports.</p></li>

AEST</span></a></div></header><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Germany’s top security official says she hopes prosecutors will find sufficient evidence to indict whomever carried out the <a href="https://apnews.com/article/russia-ukraine-germany-berlin-00232df3f4b4bc89afd47d4707724e33" data-link-name="in body link">attack on the Nord Stream gas pipelines</a> in the Baltic Sea last year.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Explosions on 26 September 2022 damaged the pipelines, which were built to carry Russian natural gas to Germany. Whom was responsible for the sabotage – which added to tensions over the <a href="https://apnews.com/hub/russia-ukraine" data-link-name="in body link">war in Ukraine</a> as European countries moved to wean themselves off Russian energy sources – <a href="https://apnews.com/article/us-germany-russia-denmark-ukraine-gas-pipeline-attack-nord-stream-2561f98ba6462db700f7609352a28c24" data-link-name="in body link">remains a mystery</a>.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Germany, <a href="https://apnews.com/article/sweden-denmark-nord-stream-gas-pipeline-explosions-ea40f35b8d96dd201a8fa75fe1db953d" data-link-name="in body link">Sweden</a> and Denmark have investigated the attack, though they have been tight-lipped about their findings.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">“I hope that the [German] federal prosecutor will find enough clues to indict the perpetrators,” the German interior minister, <strong>Nancy Faeser</strong>, said in an interview with Der Spiegel magazine published on Friday.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">“We must bring such crimes to court,” she said. “It also strengthens citizens’ confidence in the state of law when it succeeds in clearing up such complex cases.”</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">In July, European diplomats <a href="https://apnews.com/article/nord-stream-pipeline-attack-russia-investigation-4b7cb8117f420985b0d887117eebd786" data-link-name="in body link">told the UN security council</a> that investigators found traces of undersea explosives in samples taken from a yacht that was searched as part of the probe. AEST</span></a></div><h2 class="dcr-e6uddv">I urged Prigozhin to 'watch out', says Belarus leader</h2></header><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The Belarusian president, Alexander Lukashenko, said on Friday that he warned the Wagner group chiefs <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/yevgeny-prigozhin" data-link-name="in body link" data-component="auto-linked-tag">Yevgeny Prigozhin</a> and Dmitry Utkin to watch out for possible threats to their lives, and he insisted that Wagner fighters would remain in Belarus.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The Russian president, Vladimir Putin, initially vowed to crush Prigozhin’s June mutiny, comparing it to the wartime turmoil that ushered in the revolution of 1917, but hours later a deal was clinched to allow Prigozhin and some of his mercenaries to go to Belarus.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Prigozhin, Lukashenko said on Friday, had twice dismissed concerns raised by the Belarusian leader about possible threats to his life. Lukashenko said that during the mutiny he had warned Prigozhin that he would “die” if he continued to march on Moscow, to which he said Prigozhin had answered: “To hell with it – I will die.”</p><figure id="89a371aa-aead-4bb1-bb9d-f7ec6112ffe4" data-spacefinder-role="inline" data-spacefinder-type="model.dotcomrendering.pageElements.ImageBlockElement" class=" dcr-173mewl"><div AEST</span></a></div><h2 class="dcr-e6uddv">Here is a summary of today's developments:</h2></header><ul class="dcr-1kas69x">
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The Kremlin said on Friday that western suggestions that the Wagner group boss, <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/yevgeny-prigozhin" data-link-name="in body link" data-component="auto-linked-tag">Yevgeny Prigozhin</a>, had been killed on its orders were an “absolute lie”, and it declined to definitively confirm his death, citing the need to wait for test results.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Russian investigators have confirmed the death of the pilot of the plane that crashed with the loss of all onboard including Prigozhin, according to a source with knowledge of the matter.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">German prosecutors say they are investigating the attempted murder of Berlin-based Russian journalist Elena Kostyuchenko after she was one of three Russian-exile journalists who experienced symptoms consistent with poisoning.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Poland’s domestic security agency is investigating whether an outbreak of legionnaires’ disease that has killed seven people in the south of the country could be the result of intentional tampering with the water system, authorities said on Friday.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The UK’s defence ministry has said there is not yet definitive proof<strong> Prigozhin</strong> was onboard a plane that crashed with no survivors earlier this week but it is “highly likely” he is dead, Reuters reports.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The US state department on Thursday imposed sanctions on 13 people and entities it said were reportedly connected to the forced deportation and transfer of Ukraine’s children, as Washington ramps up pressure on Moscow over its invasion.</p></li>
 <li class="dcr-1kas69x"><p class="dcr-1kas69x">The United States will begin flight training for Ukrainian pilots on F-16 fighter jets in October, the Pentagon has announced.</p></li>

23.20 AEST</time></div></footer></article><article id="block-64e89eae8f081f06153f87e1" class="block dcr-1r02hz5"><header class="dcr-88va8u"><div class="dcr-1aolral"><a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2023/aug/25/russia-ukraine-war-live-updates-ukrainian-drones-launched-over-crimea-says-russia-us-to-train-f-16-pilots-in-october?page=with:block-64e89eae8f081f06153f87e1#block-64e89eae8f081f06153f87e1" data-ignore="global-link-styling" class="dcr-t8badk"><time dateTime="2023-08-25T12:31:35.000Z" data-relativeformat="med" class="dcr-1rl1qsn">6h ago</time><span class="dcr-61wgh1">22.31 AEST</span></a></div></header><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Analysts say that while the Wagner mercenary group’s brand is inevitably going to be weakened by the death of its leader, <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/yevgeny-prigozhin" data-link-name="in body link">Yevgeny Prigozhin</a>, its previous successes will serve to inspire other mercenary groups affiliated to the Russian state to emerge, albeit in a different format with likely greater Kremlin control.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">“This process may also involve rebranding, and companies within the Wagner orbit may divide into separate entities based on functional area, which may be nationalised or maintained as quasi-independent entities,” Catrina Doxsee, an associate director and associate fellow with the Transnational Threats Project at the Center for Strategic and International Studies, told AFP.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">But she added that the Russian president, Vladimir Putin, had likely seen in the June mutiny “the danger” in allowing so much power and responsibility to reside with one man.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">“Although Russia is likely to seek to continue its PMC [private military company] model for foreign policy and security assistance, it is likely that the marketplace of PMCs will diversify away from Wagner’s monopoly to prevent a repetition of Prigozhin’s challenge to the regime,” she added.</p><footer class="dcr-3i7iba"><ul class="dcr-155lzd6"><li class="dcr-16rssu9"><a AEST</span></a></div><h2 class="dcr-e6uddv">Russian investigators confirm death of pilot of downed plane and inform his family</h2></header><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Russian investigators have confirmed the death of the pilot of the plane which crashed with the loss of all on board including the mercenary chief <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/yevgeny-prigozhin" data-link-name="in body link" data-component="auto-linked-tag">Yevgeny Prigozhin</a>, according to a source with knowledge of the matter.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">They have yet to confirm a genetic match, the source added.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">An Embraer executive jet on which Prigozhin was listed as a passenger crashed in Tver region north of Moscow on 23 August, according to Russia’s Federal Air Transport Agency.</p><figure id="664d416f-eab0-4ce1-a51a-877023005055" data-spacefinder-role="inline" data-spacefinder-type="model.dotcomrendering.pageElements.ImageBlockElement" class=" dcr-173mewl"><div with a crew of three, including the pilot, Alexei Levshin.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">A source close to the situation, who spoke on condition of anonymity due to the sensitivity of the matter, told Reuters that investigators had told Levshin’s family that they had “documentary proof” he had been on the crashed plane.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Levshin’s family are due to undergo a DNA test later on Friday to establish whether they are his relatives, the source said.</p><p class="dcr-1kas69x">Investigators did not mention the fate of others registered as being on board the flight, the source
